Moved Files:
------------
Android Gradle projects use a different directory structure than ADT
Eclipse projects. Here's how the projects were restructured:

In AndroidRecording:
* AndroidManifest.xml => androidRecording\src\main\AndroidManifest.xml
* assets\ => androidRecording\src\main\assets
* libs\simplesound-0.1.jar => androidRecording\libs\simplesound-0.1.jar
* lint.xml => androidRecording\lint.xml
* res\ => androidRecording\src\main\res\
* src\ => androidRecording\src\main\java\
In ExoPlayerLib2:
* .README.txt => .readme.txt
* AndroidManifest.xml => exoPlayerLib2\src\main\AndroidManifest.xml
* assets\ => exoPlayerLib2\src\main\assets
* java\ => exoPlayerLib2\src\main\java\
* res\ => exoPlayerLib2\src\main\res\
* src\ => exoPlayerLib2\src\main\java\
In libmaterial:
* AndroidManifest.xml => libmaterial\src\main\AndroidManifest.xml
* assets\ => libmaterial\src\main\assets\
* libs\android-support-v7_2-appcompat.jar => libmaterial\libs\android-support-v7_2-appcompat.jar
* libs\nineoldandroids-2.4.0.jar => libmaterial\libs\nineoldandroids-2.4.0.jar
* res\ => libmaterial\src\main\res\
* src\ => libmaterial\src\main\java\
In libsSeekBar:

* assets\ => libsSeekBar\src\main\assets
* res\ => libsSeekBar\src\main\res\

In ExampleDrawable:

* libs\android-query-full.0.26.7.jar => exampleDrawable\libs\android-query-full.0.26.7.jar

Bugs:

If for some reason your project does not build, and you determine that
it is due to a bug or limitation of the Eclipse to Gradle importer,
please file a bug at http://b.android.com with category
Component-Tools.
